<div id="review_415144320" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/415144320" />
    <a title="Tom" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7476704-tom"><img alt="Tom" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1333052331p2/7476704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/415144320?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tom" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tom" href="/user/show/7476704-tom">Tom</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7476704-tom?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer415144320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6689946548955869703">I know that this series is hit or miss with people but it is an absolute hit with me and this book is an unwavering 5 that will go straight to the favorite’s shelf. It almost makes me want to change Lord of the Fading lands to a 4 just to distinguish how much better I felt this book was. <br/><br/>This book picks up where Lord of the Fading Lands left off. The romance dominates the story in the very beginning of the book and then there are multiple plot lines that spring up and the fantasy overtakes the r</span>
  <span id="freeText6689946548955869703" style="display:none">I know that this series is hit or miss with people but it is an absolute hit with me and this book is an unwavering 5 that will go straight to the favorite’s shelf. It almost makes me want to change Lord of the Fading lands to a 4 just to distinguish how much better I felt this book was. <br /><br />This book picks up where Lord of the Fading Lands left off. The romance dominates the story in the very beginning of the book and then there are multiple plot lines that spring up and the fantasy overtakes the romance. Gaelen’s part of the story gets integrated into the story in a more prominent role and just adds another story line to follow. The Mage’s pick up where they left off only we learn a lot more about what they are about. Of course the tension with her mother and queen Annoura was frustrating but another plot line that thickened. And then there is Ellie herself. What she is and isn’t gets revealed and we see her grow to a much greater degree in this one.<br /><br />I’m not sure how to express myself on this book. I thoroughly enjoyed it from start to finish. Ellie’s doubt about herself and being Rain’s mate is still there in the beginning of the book but from the first book till the end of this one is less than 13 days. So although I can see how it might drive people crazy, I totally could see her having reservations on everything that she was going through. Again, I don’t read fantasy for the steamy sex scenes, I usually go to PNR for that but the steamy is better in this one even if most of it is done in the mind. The villians are truly hated and the heroes are just that, heroes. The nobles still have way too much power and I would have loved for Rain to pop one of their heads off with a sneeze early on to stop how arrogant they are but Rain does get his say in the end. Ellie has to endure more than I would have liked and I wish she found her strength a little sooner than she did. Taking in the timeline of events it was all very believable her reservations of who and what she is.<br /><br />If you read the first one and liked but didn’t love it, because you felt there wasn't enough story line for a fantasy, you really should pick this up and give it a shot. Although there is plenty of places to take the story there is some finality to this one. If soul mate romance doesn’t bother you and you want an action packed fantasy with plenty of plots going on check this out.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6689946548955869703" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/133895361?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Terry (Ter05 TwiMoms/ MundieMoms)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Terry (Ter05 TwiMoms/ MundieMoms)" href="/user/show/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms">Terry (Ter05 TwiMoms/ MundieMoms)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062023698" href="/book/show/8590989-lady-of-light-and-shadows">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who loves romantic fantasy deluxe!</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Terry (Ter05 TwiMoms/ MundieMoms) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=read-more-than-once">read-more-than-once</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=could-not-put-it-down-books">could-not-put-it-down-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer133895361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6857758092562062404">Reading for the second time...in a month AWESOME AWESOME BOOK and series! I thought the first book (Lord of the Fading Lands) was great, but this second one was even better. It put new meaning into the "could not put it down" category. If you love fantasy, magic, romance, action, intrigue and great writing then I highly recommend this book, and I am on to re-read King of Sword and Sky.<br/><br/>In the first book the Tairen Soul, Rain, king of the fey, literally dropped from the sky to claim Ellysetta as h</span>
  <span id="freeText6857758092562062404" style="display:none">Reading for the second time...in a month AWESOME AWESOME BOOK and series! I thought the first book (Lord of the Fading Lands) was great, but this second one was even better. It put new meaning into the "could not put it down" category. If you love fantasy, magic, romance, action, intrigue and great writing then I highly recommend this book, and I am on to re-read King of Sword and Sky.<br /><br />In the first book the Tairen Soul, Rain, king of the fey, literally dropped from the sky to claim Ellysetta as his truemate. He has left the Fading Lands of the fey on a mission to find a way to save both the fey and the Tairen knowing that what he seeks lies in the city where he finds Ellysetta. As the mortal daughter of a woodcarver she has been fascinated with the fey all of her life, but now is thrown into a world she never dreamed of being a part of. Haunted from childhood by dreams and visions she has never understood, it is in this second book that we come to understand just what is hidden in her past and is a threat to her future.<br /><br />This author has the ability to write in a way that introduces many characters in a complex world and yet somehow it is not difficult to understand their world. The characters are amazing from the fey warrior who allows a kitten named "Love" to ride around on his shoulder because she is afraid of magic to the incredible battle scenes that use magic and physical skill in a way that you simply see it all happening. The fey in this book are simply wonderful. There is a theme among these warriors of honor, loyalty, and love that makes them so real. As fighters, they are to put it mildly, bigger than life. I find it amazing that there are so many things going on in this story including political intrigue, terrible magic ability of the mage's who plot against Allysetta for reasons one must read the book to find out, the beautiful sensual love story (and this book is NOT YA), and yet it all flows as one great tale. Goodreads friend, Stacie, was right when she said that Rain and Ellysetta are equal to Jamie and Claire as the best of all romantic couples. I tried leaving this series when I finished it a few weeks ago and just had to pick up Lord of the Fading Lands and go back to this incredible world. This is a series that I will re-read many times. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6857758092562062404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer216690435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7958380766257218237"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2011/10/review-lady-of-light-and-shadows-by-c-l-wilson.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>As the nobles of Celeria foolishly contemplate opening borders for the traitorous Eld, Rain must find a way to show that the Eld are still as evil as they were 1000 years ago and keep his soul mate Ellie safe. Ellysetta also has her own battles to face as she discovers her origins that have the power to turn her truemate Rain away from her.<br/><br/>This series just gets better and better!<br/><br/>Rain and Ellysetta are fast becoming one of my favourite romantic couples. What I like about their romance is that</span>
  <span id="freeText7958380766257218237" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2011/10/review-lady-of-light-and-shadows-by-c-l-wilson.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As the nobles of Celeria foolishly contemplate opening borders for the traitorous Eld, Rain must find a way to show that the Eld are still as evil as they were 1000 years ago and keep his soul mate Ellie safe. Ellysetta also has her own battles to face as she discovers her origins that have the power to turn her truemate Rain away from her.<br><br>This series just gets better and better!<br><br>Rain and Ellysetta are fast becoming one of my favourite romantic couples. What I like about their romance is that although it is a fated-to-be-mated plot line they still have doubts, Ellie based in her insecurity about who she is and Rain through his past experience of love the consequences of which literally scorched the world. So, although they are soul mates I like the slow build up of trust between them and watching Ellie's feeling going from hero-worship and fear to something deeper. Having said that, the first two books are set over 10 days, it just feels much longer as those days are jam packed with life altering events!<br><br>Not only do Rain and Ellie make these books for me, but the secondary characters in this also come to vivid life from C.L. Wilson's fantastic writing. Ellie's quintet of Fey, her parents, the King &amp; Queen they all have a role to play and Wilson manages to wrangle all sorts of emotions from you in this book through them.<br><br>As well as the romance between Rain and Ellie and the characters, what also draws me to this series is the pending war between the Eld and the Fey. I can't wait to see what happens next this book gives you a lot more details on the Mage's activities and I can't wait to see what happens next. I am particularly looking forward to see how Ellie is meant to heal the Tairen.<br><br>This is a great series a blend of romance and adventure, magic and swords and I can't wait to start on the next one.<br><br><b>Favourite Quote</b><br><br><i>They could not fight. They could not win. But with each moment left for them to live, they could love. That was the greatest gift the gods could ever give, and it was worth the price they would have to pay.</i></span>

<div id="review_90370430" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/90370430" />
    <a title="Gemma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2279838-gemma"><img alt="Gemma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1251085146p2/2279838.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/90370430?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gemma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gemma" href="/user/show/2279838-gemma">Gemma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2279838-gemma?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer90370430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14463145437828734182">I usually wait a day or two to review a book, just to get what I thought of it clear in my mind so that I can give a fair assessment of it. But I'm going to screw that and review this minutes after I've finished it, because all I can think right now is OMGTHATBOOKWASAMAZINGPLEASEIWANTMORE. :L<br/><br/>Honest to God, if anybody had doubts after finishing the first book, or is just thinking about reading this series, PLEASE DO SO NOW. :L<br/>I have to say, the previous book, Lord of the Fading Lands, was a littl</span>
  <span id="freeText14463145437828734182" style="display:none">I usually wait a day or two to review a book, just to get what I thought of it clear in my mind so that I can give a fair assessment of it. But I'm going to screw that and review this minutes after I've finished it, because all I can think right now is OMGTHATBOOKWASAMAZINGPLEASEIWANTMORE. :L<br /><br />Honest to God, if anybody had doubts after finishing the first book, or is just thinking about reading this series, PLEASE DO SO NOW. :L<br />I have to say, the previous book, Lord of the Fading Lands, was a little iffy for me. I mean, I adored the characters and the setting, but there were little things here &amp; there that irritated me somewhat.<br />So I started on this book, unsure what the future held for Ellie and Rain, but needing to find out. And bloody hell, I'm happy I did!<br /><br />So the first half started a little slow, &amp; I was like, 'Hmm, I totally have this figured out. When all the stuff that I just <i>know</i> is going to happen happens, I'm gonna feel so smart.' Needless to say, I was totally wrong =L<br />The last half of this book is absolutely amazing. Seriously people, I cannot remember the last time a book had me that on tenterhooks, gasping and squealing and generally in a state of hyperactivity as this book just did. The action, the excitement, the magic... It was just fantastic! Sure, there wasn't anything really original I suppose, but this book improved so much on the last one. Just when I thought I had it all figured out - Ellie's heritage, the mages, the fey - it all got turned around and around so many times I had no idea what was actually going to be the truth. And when I found out, I was like, 'OMGNOWAAAAY!' <br /><br />And just when I thought Ellie was going to get me all pissed off over the way she was unsure of Rain, Rain went and got me all worked up instead! When he turned away from Ellie, I was indignant - honestly, I probably would have broken my laptop if I had the cojones. :L<br />But what I love about this series is the feeling of hope in it; things can get really dark sometimes, and a lot of death occurs in this book, but I'm sure that the HEA will be bestowed in the end. It won't come easy, but it will come, and I can honestly say I can't wait to read the third book and finally see what the Fading Lands are like.<br />I probably would start ASAP, if not for the fact I've been up all night ooh-ing and aah-ing over this one :)<br /><br />Ellie is a great heroine - there was hardly a time when I thought what she was doing was silly, or unrealistic, something that is rare nowadays for heroines. When she finally came into her own, even what I'd hoped for was surpassed. There are still questions to be answered, and I'll just have to content myself with conjuring up theories while I try and go to sleep before I read the third book.<br /><br />I know I'm gushing, but I do not care one little bit, tbh. If you want to read something dramatic, magical, sexy &amp; addictive, read this series. It may not be the most original or best series ever written, but for entertainment &amp; sheer addiction it ranks pretty high on my list (and I have read <i>a lot</i> of books). <br />'Til next time, then - I have a feeling I'll be back here tomorrow, ranting anew about the amazing-ness of King of Sword and Sky. And frankly, I can't wait =)</span>
  <a data-text-id="14463145437828734182" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458999194" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5089951944003505951">Sometimes a book leaves you an impression because how it's written but I think that the secret of this series to me it's that it works perfectly as a means for evasion. And I was in such a need for that that from the very first moment I loved to have come back to this world and its old characters. Sometimes it reminded me of Black Jewels, a series I enjoyed a lot but they aren't comparables because this one is considerably less darker. <br/><br/>Ellysetta and Rain don't dissappoint in this one. Gaelen and</span>
  <span id="freeText5089951944003505951" style="display:none">Sometimes a book leaves you an impression because how it's written but I think that the secret of this series to me it's that it works perfectly as a means for evasion. And I was in such a need for that that from the very first moment I loved to have come back to this world and its old characters. Sometimes it reminded me of Black Jewels, a series I enjoyed a lot but they aren't comparables because this one is considerably less darker. <br><br>Ellysetta and Rain don't dissappoint in this one. Gaelen and Ellie's parents <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the real ones <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> are interesting addings and there are still a lot of characters that can offer us a lot for the rest of the series. I loved to meet Sybharukai and I'm looking forward to meet her again. <br>In this book Ellysetta will have to deal with the mess she organized at the end of the last one. I don't want to spoil anyone so I'll just say that the love and the action is much more amplified in this one. About love scenes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved the magic lessons, the wedding night much more than the beach scene. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. At the first part I was missing partly Rain's fierceness and wisdom but I got satisfied with the second half where most action is concentrated. About the action, I admit that though I couldn't put it down for about the last 40% of the book, at certain point I found that there's an intensive action scene that it was sustained for a little bit long and I was in need of a break! Anyway, I loved when a book leaves you wishing you could be able to read undisturbed and non-stop. And this one was one of those. <br>If you liked the first one, you'll probably agree that this one surpass the first one and confirms that it's a good series to finish. <br><br>PS: Do you like my black tairen? I can't take it out off my head!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787300i/493958.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer419109128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17763359748919798161"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/411341374' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lord of Fading Lands</a><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1584974.Lord_of_the_Fading_Lands__Tairen_Soul___1_' title='Lord of the Fading Lands (Tairen Soul, #1) by C.L.   <img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1185496292s/1584974.jpg' alt='Lord of the Fading Lands (Tairen Soul, #1) by C.L. Wilson' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1651313.Lady_of_Light_and_Shadows__Tairen_Soul___2_' title='Lady of Light and Shadows (Tairen Soul, #2) by C.L. Wilson' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1186377460s/1651313.jpg' alt='Lady of Light and Shadows (Tairen Soul, #2) by C.L. Wilson' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Tairen Soul Book 2</i> or more accurately <i>Tairen Soul Book 1, part 2</i> has Rain and Elysetta preparing for their impending marriage, while around them Eld mages are sowing discord within Celieria. <br/><br/>Plots abound within the Celierian nobles who are agitating for a treaty with the Eld while the peasantry are outraged over what they see as the fae killing Celierians. <br/><br/>The first half of <i>Lady of Light and Shadows</i> rates 2 Stars in my opinion. I think the author could have easily cut</span>
  <span id="freeText17763359748919798161" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/411341374" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of Fading Lands</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1584974.Lord_of_the_Fading_Lands__Tairen_Soul___1_" title="Lord of the Fading Lands (Tairen Soul, #1) by C.L. Wilson" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1185496292s/1584974.jpg" alt="Lord of the Fading Lands (Tairen Soul, #1) by C.L. Wilson" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1651313.Lady_of_Light_and_Shadows__Tairen_Soul___2_" title="Lady of Light and Shadows (Tairen Soul, #2) by C.L. Wilson" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1186377460s/1651313.jpg" alt="Lady of Light and Shadows (Tairen Soul, #2) by C.L. Wilson" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Tairen Soul Book 2</i> or more accurately <i>Tairen Soul Book 1, part 2</i> has Rain and Elysetta preparing for their impending marriage, while around them Eld mages are sowing discord within Celieria. <br><br>Plots abound within the Celierian nobles who are agitating for a treaty with the Eld while the peasantry are outraged over what they see as the fae killing Celierians. <br><br>The first half of <i>Lady of Light and Shadows</i> rates 2 Stars in my opinion. I think the author could have easily cut down the first 200 pages to two or three chapters. Calling a spade a spade, it was really boring and I could have easily walked away from it without a second thought.<br><br>The second half...happy dance.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391941ra/754645.gif" width="480" height="340" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's as good as the first half is bad. These two books together get <b>4.5 Stars</b>. I just can't rate this book on it's own.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17763359748919798161" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZAm7pyDfO0KiQxP65jWhMfW+8bVnjv4svnN4wYIbL/uiHHVBVQPo1brZCuSxEogQFIortxlyLdkXmbaxrd5XFA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('X79uP/CC70Gtx3wdcx5JM5IrBiGjT/i+sTmC8yM/406ZqqDZhV481rVdZQMkOWAScx/cI92zK0sY00yDDPqboQ==')})
  }

Before she was old enough for a marriage-of-alliance, Xylara was trained as a healer. She can\'t usurp her brother or negotiate a peace--but she can heal the brave ones injured in battle.But not only her countrymen are wounded, and Xylara\'s conscience won\'t let Firelander warriors die when she can do something to save them. She learns their language and their customs and tries to make them as comfortable as possible, despite their prisoner-of-war status.She never expects that these deeds, done in good faith, would lead to the handsome and mysterious Firelander Warlord demanding her in exchange for a cease-fire.   <span id="freeText17728676196101804320" style="display:none">C.L. Wilsons unique blend of pulse-pounding action, sweeping epic fantasy, and passionate romance has made her books a favorite read for romance and fantasy readers alike. Praised for exceptional worldbuilding and lyric prose, her critically acclaimed novels have regularly appeared on bestseller lists including the USA Today, the New York Times, and Publishers Weekly.<br /><br />C.Ls novels have won numerous industry and reader-selected awards including, LifetimeTV.coms Best Paranormal debut of 2007, the Gayle Wilson Award of Excellence, two National Readers Choice awards, the Colorado Award of Excellence, and the Holt Medallion. Ms. Wilson is the honored recipient of the PEARL award from Paranormal Romance as the best new author of 2007, and winner of the 2009 PEARL award for best Romantic Fantasy novel. <br /><br />When not torturing her characters mercilessly, C.L. enjoys relaxing with her family in sunny Florida and daydreaming of a world where people exercise in their sleep and chocolate chip cookie dough ice cream is a fat burning food.<br />"</span>
